Current Commentary 26

Water Conservancy Issues Amidst Flood Terror by Zi

In the past two weeks, the Yangtze River's water level has suddenly risen due to the summer flood season. According to recent dispatches from various locations along the river, the water level continues to rise, and the situation is becoming increasingly dangerous. People are panicked, as if the great flood of two years ago is about to reappear. During this period of terror, we journalists are loudly calling on the government to quickly mobilize all its forces to prevent disasters. The government authorities have also urgently convened flood control meetings to plan for disaster prevention. As the saying goes, "Preparedness averts peril." If rainfall does not increase in the future and the water level gradually recedes, it would be a great blessing for the residents along the river. Otherwise, even with the combined efforts of various water conservancy experts and the responsible rescue efforts of the provincial authorities, disasters will be difficult to avoid, and sacrifices may only be slightly reduced. However, the current terror has not yet ended, and future disasters are still worrisome. Today, we must carefully study the issue of Yangtze River water conservancy. Water conservancy experts, based on the historical records of the Yangtze River water level, believe that a high record is reached approximately every ten years and hope that this year will not result in a disaster. However, in fact, only two years have passed since the great flood of the 20th year of the Republic of China, and the water level in places like Hankou is already higher than it was during the same period back then. Zhu Yongjun, the head of the Public Works Section of the Economic Commission, said, "In ancient times, competing with water for land was strictly prohibited. In the 20th year of the Republic of China, the National Government also proposed returning farmland to lakes. However, people do not weigh the advantages and disadvantages and build small dikes outside the main dikes built by the Flood Disaster Committee. Dikes are like nets between Dongting and Poyang, turning the sea into mulberry fields. Without adequate outlets for the water, it is difficult to prevent disasters." Therefore, the most recent cause of the high water level is the residents living near the lakes occupying the lakes for farmland, reducing the outlet for the river water. The section of the Yangtze River from Yichang to Hankou has always been the area most prone to flooding. The river flows down from Jingmen, out of Huya, and onto the plain with great force. In the past, the meandering river channels and the obstruction of long dikes hindered its discharge, causing "the troubles of the Yangtze to lie in Chu." After the huge sacrifices of the 20th year, the meandering river channels remain, the densely distributed sandbars remain, the tributaries have not been smoothed, and the capacity of the lakes to absorb and release water has not increased. Instead, the trend of occupying lakes for farmland has greatly increased, causing this great disaster. The disaster is self-inflicted and cannot be attributed to natural causes.

The world's most skilled country in water management is the Netherlands. The Dutch compete with natural forces, conquering the sea and blocking raging waves to prevent them from causing harm. Today, the cause of the Yangtze River's flooding is self-inflicted by the people living near the river. Residents only know their own small interests, enclosing wasteland to create private property, without considering the resulting flood disaster. The property and lives of others will be sacrificed. The government can only panic temporarily, blocking water and rushing to rescue, clinging to the Buddha in a crisis, without paying attention to fundamental water conservancy facilities. After the huge flood disaster of the 20th year, and now with this current terror, can they learn a lesson?

The Situation at the World Economic Conference is Again Chaotic 27

The US's Nationalistic Policy of Stabilizing Currency Has Failed

The British Prime Minister Expresses Willingness to Work Towards Reconciliation to Finally Achieve a Currency Truce

(London) The declaration issued yesterday by the US delegation that a temporary currency stabilization plan is currently untimely has thrown the World Economic Conference into a state of disarray. Today, the situation remains the same. All parties acknowledge the failure to establish a currency stabilization plan with the US. The most serious aspect of the situation is the talk of postponing the current conference, but this is not favored by official circles. The British side hopes that the current intransigence is only temporary and that internal conditions will improve in a few weeks, making a compromise possible. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd) (London) The sharp conflict between the French and American delegations regarding the issue of currency stabilization still exists. France is demanding that the US agree to immediate partial stabilization, but the US delegation seems to still be awaiting instructions from the US President. French Finance Minister Bonnet has stated that a currency stabilization agreement must be concluded before all other agreements, and explained that the urgency of concluding this agreement has led to the recent resurgence of rumors that France intends to abandon the gold standard if the exchange rate of the US dollar is not firm. This rumor has affected all major securities markets in the world, causing prices to fluctuate. However, the French delegation has remained silent on this rumor. The French representative also pointed out that the US's refusal to agree to immediate stabilization has left the world's currency prices in the hands of speculators. However, the US representative did not want to comment on this. In short, at present, within the Economic Conference, only the silver issue has made progress. Other issues are still waiting for the right moment. The time when agreements on tariffs and other trade barriers can be reached is likely still far away. (National Telegram, 22nd)

(London) US officials claim that a temporary currency stabilization plan is currently untimely. The atmosphere surrounding the difficult issue of currency stabilization at the World Economic Conference has been slightly clarified by this statement. According to members of the US official circle, temporary stabilization may cause a sharp drop in prices, which would defeat the US's plan to raise prices. The US official circle also revealed that the US has submitted a proposal advocating a consistent monetary policy to promote economic activity and increase prices to achieve the ultimate stability of unstable currencies. The US official circle's release of this statement after receiving secret instructions from Washington shows that President Roosevelt has officially begun a nationalistic policy. However, it is heard that the US delegation, because France attaches great importance to currency stability, will use currency stability as a tool for future negotiations until other economic plans have been considered. (Reuters dispatch, 22nd)

(London) British Prime Minister MacDonald told reporters this afternoon that greater momentum and internal strength must be injected into the World Conference, as was done in the first week. Next week, the third week, will be a period for all parties to do their best to reconcile with each other. This should make everyone aware of the importance of the work ahead. International conferences often become pessimistic in the second week, but the World Economic Conference is not like that this week, he said. MacDonald continued, "I am now optimistic as we enter the third week. In the past, I felt somewhat discouraged when the fate of the Lausanne Conference was uncertain, but that is not the case today." There have been some setbacks in the past week, especially regarding the hope for temporary currency stabilization, but this is not a major concern. The US's position is indeed difficult. The US is currently engaged in raising its domestic prices. Anything at the conference that could hinder the rise in prices is not something the US wants. The situation after yesterday is neither completely gloomy nor without any certainty. The talk of postponing the conference is foolish, as this would only lead to the conference breaking up. Nothing could have a worse impact on the determination of countries to find a solution. The excessive workload of the secretariat is only a minor obstacle, as there is much to be done and the secretariat's organization is insufficient to cope with it. During consultations in subcommittees, all parties can still exchange views on currency stabilization. When we reach a stage of mutual understanding and cooperation, we will see that the conference has value in continuing to meet. MacDonald concluded his speech with a sincere attitude: "We must revive our spirit of action, and we must have the driving force." (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

The Memorandum Carried by Moley to England is Penned by Baruch 28

(Washington) The memorandum carried by Moley to England was drafted by US Presidential Advisor Baruch, detailing the relationship between the US situation and the World Economic Conference, so that Moley can use it freely in the conference. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Roosevelt's Policies Receive Support from Domestic Farmers 29

But Business and Industry Are Not Very Supportive

(Washington) The US President's nationalistic method of supporting the recovery of industry and commerce, in contrast to Europe's plan to encourage industry and commerce through international cooperation, seems to have created a deadlock at the Economic Conference. Recently, more and more people have held this view. Some newspapers claim that the President, even if he wants to cooperate enthusiastically in London, is still determined to maintain the gains he has made domestically using purely nationalistic methods. According to financial circles, the recent rise in commodity securities is mostly due to the devaluation of the gold standard. Once this artificially inflated price falls, it is feared that it will cause political turmoil. Currently, the strongest supporters of the US President are the farmers, who have greatly benefited from the inflated currency plan and the artificial raising of prices. In addition, although prices have risen, wages have not increased correspondingly, and the number of unemployed has not decreased correspondingly. Therefore, the President's intention is to maintain the support of the farmers at this time. Today, agricultural groups in Washington all support the US delegation's declaration in London, believing that the US's raising of prices domestically will be more beneficial to the world than agreeing to temporary exchange rate stabilization. However, according to Wall Street sources, the banking and manufacturing industries have not been able to endorse this attitude, believing that continuing to prepare to use nationalistic methods to revive industry and commerce cannot be reconciled with efforts to achieve international cooperation. It is expected that if an agreement cannot be reached in London that is consistent with the methods used by the President to date, then the President will retreat and implement a nationalistic economic policy, relying on his extensive powers to protect domestic industry and commerce. Furthermore, although the value of the gold standard has fallen in the past two days, the prices of securities and commodities have still fallen due to the uncertainty of the situation at the London Conference. Observers in New York are concerned about this decline, fearing that once the artificially inflated prices fall, political turmoil will follow. (National Telegram, 22nd)

France Denies Abandoning the Gold Standard 30

(London) There are rumors in both New York and London that France will abandon the gold standard. The French delegation to the World Economic Conference has denied this, saying that the news is completely fabricated. (Havas dispatch, 22nd)

London Opinion is Greatly Disappointed 31

(London) It is heard that various morning newspapers are greatly disappointed with the suggestions made by the United States yesterday (i.e., abolishing artificial trade barriers). The Times stated that most delegations regarded currency stabilization as the primary mission. The newspaper stated, "The devaluation of currency is too great to allow prices to rise in the same proportion as the US dollar. The drop in prices is already irreversible. If currency continues to depreciate, then the drop in prices should be even greater than it is today." The Times financial supplement stated that people in financial circles believe that if the currency stabilization problem cannot be resolved for even a day, then the World Economic Conference will not have any effect for even a day. Some even advocate temporarily postponing the Economic Conference until the fall, and having a committee carry out preparatory work in the meantime. (Havas News Agency dispatch, 22nd)

MacDonald Receives Litvinov 32

British-Russian Trade Negotiations Revived

(London) Today, British Prime Minister MacDonald held a tea party. Soviet Russian representative Litvinov attended with his wife. The hope for British-Russian negotiations is thus revived, as the British ban on Russian imports and the imprisonment of two British employees of Vickers Company in Russia both need to be resolved. The Russian authorities previously accused the two British employees of Vickers Company of espionage and sabotage and sentenced them to two to three years of imprisonment on April 18. The British authorities considered this unfair and retaliated by banning Russian imports. This is why Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov issued sarcastic remarks during the opening of the Economic Conference. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

(London) Attention is being paid here to British Prime Minister MacDonald's invitation to Soviet Russian Foreign Commissar Litvinov and eleven others to a luncheon this afternoon. Litvinov told reporters before attending the banquet that Soviet Russia would only consider releasing the imprisoned two British engineers after Britain cancelled the ban on trade with Russia. It is now believed that the British Prime Minister will first launch talks on the issue of ending the British-Russian trade war during the luncheon. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Work of the Two Committees 33

(Currency and Silver Group)

Nine Countries Form a Special Committee

To Negotiate a Plan to Stabilize Silver Prices

(London) Today, the Silver Group Committee of the Currency Committee spent the entire day in detailed and frank discussions of the draft proposal submitted by US representative Pittman. It was felt that an understanding between the major silver-producing countries and the countries storing large amounts of silver was a necessary condition for the success of the agreement. During today's meeting, a special committee was established. Representatives from the United States, Mexico, Canada, Argentina, Peru, and Bolivia handled the adjustment of the silver supply, and representatives from China, India, and Spain considered the issue of restricting the flow of government silver reserves into the market. (Reuters dispatch, 22nd)

(London) An agreement to stabilize silver prices between the major silver-producing countries and silver-storing countries is expected to begin drafting soon. The Silver Subcommittee has nominated a special committee to negotiate a detailed stabilization plan, which will be submitted to the Subcommittee for approval and then transferred to the plenary session of the conference. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Ma Yinchu Talks About Raising Silver Prices 34

(Nanjing) During the World Economic Conference, the silver issue is also an important case for discussion. Central News Agency reporters believe that the silver issue is most closely related to our country. On the 23rd, they interviewed Ma Yinchu, Chairman of the Finance Committee of the Legislative Yuan, for his opinion. According to Ma, the great powers want to raise silver prices and will inevitably abandon the gold standard and inflate the currency in order to restore world economic prosperity, and then silver prices will rise. However, according to economic trends, the cycle of successive panic is still likely to reappear one day, and silver prices will eventually fall again. (Central News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

(Currency Stabilization Group)

Discussing the European Debt Problem 35

(London) The Stabilization Subcommittee of the Currency Committee of the World Economic Conference met this afternoon to discuss the debt problem. French Finance Minister Bonnet, the rapporteur of the Currency Committee, chaired the meeting on behalf of Italian Finance Minister Jung. The Hungarian representative, Imredy, argued that a compromise should be reached with foreign governments and foreign creditors so that creditor countries could directly revise debts through judicial means. The Romanian Finance Minister requested a change in debt contracts to reduce debt immediately and permanently. The Turkish representative argued that agreements should be signed between creditor and debtor countries to repay debts in kind. The Ecuadorian delegation hoped to establish an international public fund to allow countries to re-borrow. The Greek representative argued that commercial agreements should be signed between major creditor countries and small debtor countries. (Havas dispatch, 22nd)

Economic Committee 36

(London) The main committee of the Economic Conference met today, chaired by British Prime Minister MacDonald, to review the inertia of the Economic Conference. It is generally believed that the two committees on currency and brokerage will continue to discuss tomorrow, but the final agreement must wait until the US dollar is finally stabilized before it can be established. The first session of the Economic Conference seems to be proceeding until July. The second session may be delayed until October so that the two committees can take advantage of the interval to remove obstacles to the conference. It is generally hoped that the examination of the US currency inflation policy will be completed before the second session opens. The reason for delaying this meeting is that the United States expressed its opposition to stabilizing the currency this morning. (Havas dispatch, 23rd)

British Business Minister Appointed Rapporteur 37

(London) British Business Minister Hore-Belisha was appointed today as the rapporteur of the Economic and Trade Committee of the World Economic Conference. (Reuters dispatch, 22nd)

Proposals for Production and Sales Should Be Flexible 38

(London) The subcommittee discussing production and sales issues in the Economic Committee has decided that any plans or drafts submitted to the Economic Subcommittee regarding reorganization issues should have considerable flexibility in order to include various subsidiary and associated products. Such plans or drafts should obtain the consent of the general producing countries, and within each producing country, the majority of producers should approve them. The approach should be fair to both producers and consumers and should be sufficiently effective to make all parties feel safe. The above principles are influenced by the declaration of British Colonial Secretary Lister. (Havas dispatch, 22nd)

US Representative Proposes Practical Measures to Revive Trade 39

(London) US representative Coulson today proposed practical measures to revive trade and raise prices, advocating close cooperation between governments on central bank policies to provide sufficient credit and advocating the promotion of employment with government funds and the placement of the unemployed. Coulson also said that the way to promote world recovery should be sought through simultaneous programs of government spending in various countries on parallel lines. These programs must be designed to encourage natural sources that provide employment, restore industry and commerce, and restore the willingness of private individuals to take on ordinary commercial risks. Coulson also argued that banks of various countries should meet to immediately discuss everything. (Reuters dispatch, 22nd)

Irish Representative Attacks British Punitive Tariffs 40

(London) Today, the representative of the Irish Free State launched a major attack on Britain's commercial policy in the Trade Tariff Subcommittee of the World Economic Conference. He claimed that Britain, for revenge, deliberately destroyed the economy of the Free State and attempted to overthrow the government of the Free State. Therefore, if hostility between Britain and Ireland is to persist forever, then the so-called tariff coordinator will never have any hope of existing. For the sake of world economic independence, such tariffs used by large countries to punish small countries must be announced at the World Economic Conference. After publicly attacking the British government, the Irish representative dispersed his speech to reporters, and the atmosphere in the meeting hall became very tense for a while, because the debate of the various countries' agreement subcommittees should be treated as a secret discussion. (National Telegram, 22nd)

German Representative Hugenberg Will Not Return to London 41

(London) German Economic Minister Hugenberg was one of the German representatives who attended the World Economic Conference a few days ago, but according to informed sources at the World Economic Conference, Hugenberg will not return to London. The situation in the German political situation is still the main material discussed at the conference. It is expected that Hugenberg will soon resign from the post of Economic Minister. As for Hugenberg's proposal submitted to the conference to recover the German territory, it was officially withdrawn two days ago, at which time Germany had dissolved the domestic National Rights Party organization. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

Our Representative Proposes to the International Labor Conference 42

Industrial and Commercial Enterprises Inside and Outside Concessions

Should Abide by Chinese Labor Regulations

Indian Representative Asks to Intervene in the India-Japan Tariff War

(Geneva) Chinese representative Xiao Jirong to the International Labor Conference today presented a resolution, arguing that the Conference should ask the administration group to consult with the governments concerned to guarantee that all Chinese and foreign industrial and commercial enterprises in the concessions and leased territories should abide by Chinese labor regulations. (Reuters dispatch, 22nd) (Geneva) Indian representative Taybally today asked the International Labor Organization to intervene in the India-Japan tariff war at the International Labor Conference, saying that Japan's low wages have contributed to India's reduction in wages and general defensive policies, especially in the cotton textile industry. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Fifty-Six Countries Worldwide Participate in the Tariff Truce 43

(London) Yugoslavia has approved the tariff truce, so the signatories to this truce have reached fifty-six countries. Only eleven countries have not yet participated. (Havas dispatch, 22nd)

Nankai University Student Jumps to His Death After Failing Exam

Most of the Yi Shui Society Members Disbanded

After the Establishment of the Four-Power Pact, Mussolini Launched the Danube Economic Alliance

Rumors of Austro-Hungarian Restoration Are Rife

Reuters, Paris, 22nd - Officials here today dismiss recent rumors about plans to restore the Austro-Hungarian monarchy, saying that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has never sought Paris's opinion on this matter. In fact, what he seeks is a form of economic agreement, wanting to include the Danube countries in an association of good fellowship. The second step, of course, would be a meeting between French Prime Minister Daladier and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, but this meeting may not be realized in a short time.

Reuters, Budapest, 22nd - Rumors that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has proposed plans to the major powers to restore the Austro-Hungarian monarchy have been dismissed by officials here today as unfounded. They claim that Hungarian Prime Minister Gombos recently stated that such a federation belonging to the past is not what Hungary needs, and the whole country agrees with this statement.

Havas, Paris, 22nd - Rumors that Italy and France are currently discussing plans for a Hungarian-Austrian union have been denied by French officials. Paris Evening Post published an article commenting on the matter, saying that France has always been closely associated with the Little Entente countries. If it promotes Hungarian-Austrian rapprochement, then France's views will deviate from those of the Little Entente countries, which is definitely not what Foreign Minister Pang Gu wants to do. According to the views of French political figures, the only way to organize Central Europe is to establish a broad economic compromise, allowing all countries in the Danube region to join.

Havas, London, 22nd - Those close to the Hungarian delegation to the London Economic Conference have firmly denied rumors that Hungary is currently considering restoration. British officials said that foreign rumors that Italian diplomatic authorities have contacted the British Foreign Office regarding the Hungarian-Austrian union issue are not true. The United Kingdom is in a dilemma regarding this matter: one is to allow Hungary to restore the monarchy and unite with Austria, and the other is to allow Germany and Austria to unite. However, the general public trusts Austria, saying that it will definitely be able to defend its independence and will not unite with Germany. However, Austria's attitude may not last long. The United Kingdom seems to intend to advocate an economic construction plan, so that the countries formed after the division of the former Austro-Hungarian Empire can unite economically and maintain their political autonomy.

Havas, Paris, 23rd - Foreign Minister Pang Gu met with Yugoslav Foreign Minister Yefudichu. After the meeting, Yefu said that the matters discussed were related to the Central European issue. When asked about the Habsburg royal family's restoration movement in Hungary, Yefu replied that this matter was not mentioned.

National News, Paris, 23rd - According to a report from Rome, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is now urging German Chancellor Hitler, French Prime Minister Daladier, and British Prime Minister MacDonald to come to Rome to sign the Four-Power Pact. The date will be around mid-next month.

Hitler's Reaction

Reuters, Berlin, 23rd - All Christian trade unions in Germany cease to exist from today. Dr. Lai, the national commissioner for the protection of workers' interests, has issued an order to expel all former leaders of Christian trade unions and replace them with figures from the National Socialist Party. This is the second order from Germany interfering in workers' organizations. The first order was issued on May 2nd, temporarily confiscating the bank accounts of free trade unions for investigation. At that time, Dr. Lai stated that the National Socialist Party must take over the trade unions to protect the interests of workers. All Christian and other non-socialist trade unions must also recognize the new order, otherwise they will be dissolved. The government's goal is to unify all associations.

Reuters, Berlin, 22nd - The Socialist Party within Germany is now suffering a severe blow. One hundred and twenty Socialist Party members of parliament, state parliaments, and city councils have been ordered to be suspended from their positions and immediately cease receiving salaries. Socialist Party gatherings and newspapers have been banned, and the party's property and funds have also been confiscated. At the same time, the government has ordered that all civil servants are not allowed to join the Socialist Party from today. The government announced today that the German Socialist Party has absolute evidence of a conspiracy to overthrow the government, and claimed that the leaders of the Socialist Party have plans to resist the government. Prussian Interior Minister Goering today instructed all federal governments to take the same steps against the Socialist Party to protect the people and the country.

National News, Berlin, 22nd - In recent days, the government has collected various information from independent sources, proving that the Social Democratic Party is indeed continuing its treasonous activities. Therefore, it has been decided to dissolve the party as a whole and prohibit it from reorganizing. The Social Democratic Party members in parliament will also be removed from their positions. All propaganda materials and gatherings of the party will be banned, and the newspapers and journals belonging to the party will be permanently suspended. All party fees will be confiscated, and all civil servants will not be allowed to belong to the party in the future.

National News, Berlin, 22nd - According to a news agency related to Hu Zhenpei, Hu claimed that he still cannot agree with the reasons given by the government for dissolving the Fenmen Corps. He has expressed his position to certain important figures. According to the Berlin Daily News, this statement was clearly allowed to be published by Hu. This proves that there is an extraordinary plan outside the cabinet to deal with the Fenmen Corps. However, the opinions among the cabinet members are very different and difficult to reconcile.

Reuters, Munich, 23rd - The tombstones of Eisner, who was the prime minister when the Bavarian Communist Party came to power in 1919, and Landauer, the Communist Party leader who was shot, were all destroyed today in accordance with the orders of the city council. The ashes of the two men will be preserved by Jewish religious leaders. The city council announced the reason for this, saying that it had recently been discovered that someone was plotting to blow up Eisner's tomb. Eisner was a famous journalist and wrote many books on art, drama, and sociology. He gained fame at the Berlin Academy of Philosophy and Germanic Literature. In his youth, he wrote "Nietzsche's Doctrine," which was highly regarded. From 1892, he worked as a reporter for the Frankfurter Zeitung. In 1897, he was sentenced to nine months in prison for promoting socialism. At the end of the European War, he organized a bloodless civil revolution in Bavaria. After King Ludwig abdicated, he served as prime minister. In early 1919, he was killed by Spartacist soldiers. His book "The Sultan of World War" predicted the World War.

Japan Asks the UK for Opinions on Negotiations with India

Dentsu, Tokyo, 23rd - This morning, Foreign Minister Uchida consulted with the heads of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the issue of Japanese-Indian trade. As a result, he will send the following telegram to Ambassador Matsudaira in the UK, proposing that Japan and India begin direct negotiations and questioning the UK government's true intentions. The Japanese government hopes that official diplomatic negotiations will begin in Shimla by representatives of Japan and India. Does the UK government intend to give the Indian government the authority to negotiate this matter? What is the nature of the confirmation that the UK government will give as a result of the negotiations? Because the negotiations must be extensive, the Japanese government hopes that the UK government will reply quickly.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 23rd - The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs attaches importance to whether the UK government's confirmation of the results of the Japanese-Indian negotiations is formal or substantive. Therefore, it has telegraphed Ambassador Matsudaira in the UK separately. If it is substantive, the negotiations in Shimla may be overturned in London. Therefore, the UK government's reply will have a great impact on the future of the Japanese-Indian issue and deserves close attention.

Japan Alliance News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd - The Japanese government has decided to appoint Minister Sawada as the chief representative for the negotiations on the Japanese-Indian issue, and Director Takeuchi of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry and Consul-General Miyake stationed in India as representatives. The order to depart will be issued in mid-July, and the negotiations will begin in early August.

Japan Establishes Transportation Conference, Close Liaison Between the Navy and Army

Dentsu, Tokyo, 23rd - Today's regular cabinet meeting was held at the Prime Minister's official residence at 10 a.m. All cabinet members attended except for Naval Minister Osumi. Army Minister Araki explained the establishment of the Transportation Conference, saying that it would not be based on the budget or official system, but a committee would be established by the relevant ministries to hold meetings. The results would be reviewed and decided by the cabinet. After discussions, it was decided to establish a transportation conference to establish fundamental policies for overall transportation. Because the relevant ministries must take contact, it was officially decided to establish a transportation conference. The cabinet will draft a concrete plan for its organization, staffing, and other specific details.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 23rd - The administrative vice-ministers of each ministry held a meeting at the Prime Minister's official residence yesterday to discuss the establishment of the Transportation Conference proposed by Army Minister Araki. As a result, it was decided that the Railway Conference and Civil Engineering Conference would remain in existence, and a large-scale Transportation Conference would be established above them. The specific plan will be drafted by the Legal Bureau.

Japan Alliance News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd - Yesterday, the administrative vice-ministers of each ministry discussed the establishment of the Transportation Conference advocated by Army Minister Araki. According to Army Minister Araki's original proposal, a unified transportation conference would be established to link the various transportation facilities under the jurisdiction of each ministry, with the aim of establishing a comprehensive national defense transportation policy for the army, navy, and air force. As a result of the exchange of opinions among the vice-ministers, they all expressed their agreement. However, the following specific methods will be submitted to the Legal Bureau for preparation as soon as possible and submitted to the next meeting for decision: (1) How to deal with the existing railway, civil engineering, and other conferences in terms of their existence and authority after the establishment of the Transportation Conference; (2) How to deal with the funding issue; the second reserve fund for this year has been exhausted, and should it be included in the new budget for next year; (3) How should the organization and organization methods of this agency be structured; should the Prime Minister be appointed as the chairman or should transportation experts be sought from the government and private sectors; (4) Should it be a permanent agency.

British Non-War Movement

National News, Edinburgh, 22nd - After a heated debate today, the British League of Nations Union passed all resolutions opposing world war. Because the chairman of the association is Sir Cecil, the resolutions passed this time are particularly important. According to the resolution, British soldiers in the army, navy, and air force can refuse to obey the orders of their superiors during wartime if the war has been deemed illegal by the League of Nations. The resolution was initially proposed by a small number of people, but it was passed by a large majority of 290 votes to 10 votes. However, Cecil believed that this resolution seemed to encourage betrayal in the army. Therefore, he wanted to propose another solution, that is, all members of the British League of Nations Union should use the power of legal means to prevent the progress of such a war when they encounter an illegal war, and at the same time refuse any actions that support this war. This resolution was also passed unanimously.

Wah Lih Shih Umbrella Shop

Former Police Officer Ma Wenxiang Commits Suicide by Train Due to Patriotic Concerns

Unable to Reconcile Loyalty and Filial Piety, He Chooses Death

His Hatred for the Japanese Remains Unassuaged Despite Hand-to-Hand Combat

Ma Wenxiang, a 29-year-old native of Dongchang Prefecture, Shandong Province, previously served as a second-class police officer in the third squad of the second company of the Municipal Police Bureau, stationed in Caoh Jing Town in western Shanghai. Ma was known for his honesty, filial piety, and bravery. In the autumn of 1930, he invited his father, Ma Haoyou, 57 years old, who had only Wenxiang as his child, to come to Shanghai. After arriving in Shanghai, Ma Haoyou was introduced to work as a janitor at the New Longhua Hui Ling English School. Before the January 28th Incident two years ago, the squad was ordered to move to the front lines in Zhabei. Ma also participated in the resistance against the Japanese, engaging in hand-to-hand combat for a week. Eventually, he was transferred to the Bund and Caojiadu, among other locations. Last autumn, the squad was ordered to reorganize, and Ma subsequently retired and returned home, living with his father at the Hui Ling School in western Shanghai. At that time, the Japanese were invading Manchuria, and Wenxiang repeatedly expressed his desire to go north to join the volunteer army to fight the enemy. However, his elderly father refused, and he was unable to fulfill his wish, causing him great frustration. He became depressed and fell ill, remaining bedridden for several months until this spring. Wenxiang was aware that the eastern provinces had been lost and North China was in turmoil. He made a second request to his father, but his father questioned who would care for him in his old age. Wenxiang had no choice but to give up, but he sighed and lamented all day, often singing that he could not reconcile loyalty and filial piety. The students at the school ridiculed him. In March, Wenxiang attempted suicide by drowning but was rescued by fellow villagers and survived. However, his old illness relapsed, causing a nervous breakdown. After undergoing several treatments, he recovered last month. When Wenxiang was stationed in Zhabei during the tense war, he still took leave to visit his father, so his father loved him very much. The father and son did not want to be separated. Last week, Haoyou handed over his job at the school to Wenxiang and went to work as a cook at the Second Prison in Caohejing. Unexpectedly, Wenxiang went out alone around 9 PM on the evening before last (June 22nd) and committed suicide on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway in front of the Xinzhai Gate (about 200 yards northwest of the Hui Ling School, the same location where Gai Jianye, a graduate of Hui Ling High School, committed suicide on the morning of June 24, 1931). He was discovered yesterday morning, having been crushed to death by a night express train at 10:30 PM the night before. His left foot was severed, and his body was dismembered, a gruesome sight to behold. When reporters heard the news and drove to the countryside to investigate, the body was still lying on the muddy road north of the railway track, and the father of the deceased, Ma Haoyou, was weeping beside it. The old man's lamentations were heartbreaking. He provided the reporter with details about the deceased's life, noting that his aspirations were commendable, and his situation was indeed distressing. Yang Xinzheng, a municipal affairs committee member in the district, took pity on him and provided a coffin. The body was collected at 5 PM. The father of the deceased reported the matter to the Sixth District Third Sub-Bureau, requesting an exemption from an autopsy.

Li Guojie's Judgment 47

Meanwhile, Li has retained lawyer Zhang Yipeng and filed another appeal to the Supreme Court. The full text of the Jiangsu High Court Criminal Judgment (21st Year Su Zi No. 1742) is as follows:

(Judgment) Appellant Li Guojie, male, 53 years old, native of Hefei County, Anhui Province, resident of 1005 Avenue Joffre, Shanghai, former General Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. (Defense Attorneys) Lawyer Zhang Yiguan, Lawyer Jiang Yiping, Lawyer Zhang Shijian.

The Truth About the Large-Scale Electricity Theft by the Above-Mentioned Appellant and Colluding Mechanics 50

Electric Meter Seals Were Replicated by a Returned Engineer from Japan 51

The Replicated Seals Were Indistinguishable from the Original Seals │The Numbers Could Be Removed and Adjusted at Will││Internal and External Collusion Made the Case Complex│ 52

Recently, the Shanghai Power Company discovered that some users were colluding with mechanics to engage in large-scale electricity theft. The company reported this to the police station, requesting an investigation. Under the supervision of Chief Inspector Lu Liankui of the General Investigation Department, detectives Shao Jingfan, Zhou Honglin, Wang Hongsheng, Deng Shu, and others conducted a thorough investigation, uncovering the secrets involved and making arrests. Cheng Zhangcai from Pudong, Zhang Yulin, Liu Zhaoji, Huang Youliang, Xu Jinling, and 13 others were arrested. Various important pieces of evidence were seized. Last Tuesday, seven people, including Lu Qinghong, were released after an investigation proved they were not involved. Cheng Zhangcai and the other five were handed over to the First Special District Court. After Chief Inspector Lu launched his own investigation, he discovered that, apart from Liu Zhaoji, who was a coppersmith, the rest were employees of the Power Company. Since the factories and businesses used a considerable amount of electricity, resulting in high monthly electricity bills, they colluded with Cheng and others to tamper with the electric meters.

When the electric meters were installed by the Power Company, two lead seals were used to secure the screws on the meter casing. If these lead seals were broken, it would be easy to dismantle the meter. Therefore, these two lead seals served as a lock for the electric meter. Once the meter was dismantled, the numbers could be removed and adjusted at will, either forward or backward. While lead pellets were easy to make, lead seals were difficult to replicate. One side of the lead seal had the words "Western Power Company" in English, and the other side had the number "15". Once tampered with, it would break and could not be restored. Fortunately, one of the accomplices, Zhou Dikang, who had not yet been apprehended, had studied engineering in Japan and returned to China. He was able to replicate the lead seals perfectly.

Thus, he produced a type of lead seal that was indistinguishable from the real one. Cheng and others then began to commit their crimes. Because the amount of electricity used varied, and the Power Company's meter reading dates were unpredictable, they colluded with one or two employees within the Power Company who were specifically responsible for this task. These employees would report the situation in advance, making their method of committing the crime very meticulous and difficult to detect. Various factories and businesses had their meters tampered with.

For example, if a factory's monthly electricity usage was 400 units, Cheng and others could change the reading to 200 units. The factory would then pay 200 units less in electricity bills and give Cheng and others a small reward. Both parties benefited. This type of behavior had been going on for a long time without being discovered due to the high skill of the meter tampering. It was not easy to uncover the crime, but now it has been exposed. It has been discovered that Cheng and others had tampered with the meters of countless factories. Among them, there was sufficient evidence to prosecute the following (more than 20 companies): (1) Tianwei Textile Factory at 15 Lane 296 Rue Tenant de la Tour; (2) Guohua Silk Factory at 417 Rue Tenant de la Tour; (3) Oriental Silk Factory at 50-54 Yulin Road; (4) Hengfeng Silk Factory at 65 Yulin Road; (5) Qingxing Silk Factory on Yulin Road; (6) Youfeng Silk Factory at 42 Yulin Road; (7) Weiwen Silk Factory on Yangzhou Road; (8) Shenyi Silk Factory at 109 Huasheng Road; (9) Yuandong Silk Factory at 44 Tao Peng Road; (10) Jinya Silk Factory at 46 Tao Peng Road; (11) Huada Silk Factory at 578 Connaught Road; (12) Hengda Department Store at 432 Route Boppe; (13) Shuxin Silk Factory on Weihaiwei Road; (14) China Store at 244 Nanking Road; (15) Dahua Department Store at 430 Nanking Road; (16) Zhenchang Dyeing Factory at 271 Fuzhou Road; (17) Xinwei Silk Factory at 998 Route Cardinal Mercier; (18) Yuandong Silk Factory at 232 Tangshan Road; (19) Yongtai Electroplating Company at 159 Beihai Road; (20) Taixing Company on Rehe Road; (21) Meifeng Silk Factory at 152 Tongzhou Road; (22) Jiuchun Silk Factory at 85 Hart Road; (23) Hefengrongji Silk Factory at 272 Rue Hellé; (24) Meicheng Silk Factory at 1145 Dong Youheng Road. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Feng Shide of the First Special District Court (Criminal Division One) opened the court for questioning. Lawyer Ru Baoyi represented the police station and stated the above situation. The defendants were defended by lawyers Fan Gang, Lin Yingqing, Shen Xingxia, and Lu Qi. The police station reiterated the previous situation and stated that they were prosecuting the defendants under Article 338, Section 7 of the Criminal Law for habitual theft, Article 340, Section 2 for stealing electricity, and Article 234 for forgery of seals. Western detective Hunter testified about the circumstances under which the defendants were arrested and the forged seals and documents were seized. Representatives from the Power Company, foreigners Mayer and Kfu, explained the structure of the electric meter and the methods of cheating. When questioned, the defendants generally confessed. After the judge repeatedly interrogated the witnesses and defendants, he announced that the case would be adjourned for further hearing.

Due to a case of embezzlement, an appeal was filed against the first instance judgment of the Shanghai District Court on December 27, 1932. This court, upon review, renders the following judgment:

(Main Text) The original judgment regarding Li Guojie is revoked. Li Guojie is sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment for intending to illegally possess public property for a third party, with deprivation of civil rights for five years. The number of days of pre-trial detention shall be credited against the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. The remaining charges are dismissed.

(Facts) Li Guojie was originally the chairman of the board of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. In March 1932, he was appointed as the general manager of the company by the Ministry of Communications. Due to the company's poor business performance, he sought to reorganize it. He planned to repay old debts, redeem mortgaged assets, add ships, build docks, and expand business. He contacted the American China Business Corporation to negotiate construction loan and dock loan agreements, totaling Shanghai taels 10 million. In addition, he entered into a contract to purchase ships on credit. These were all approved by Chen Fumu, the Vice Minister of Communications and Supervisor of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. On September 5th and 6th of the same year, Li Guojie and the Business Corporation withheld the above loan agreements. Fearing that the loan would fail, Li Guojie, on the 23rd of the same month, unilaterally withdrew 700,000 taels of the loan from the Business Corporation and handed it over to Huang Jusu, the representative sent by Chen Fumu. The money was not recorded in the accounting books, with the intention of making it up gradually when the business improved. At the same time, Chen Fumu returned the loan agreement. Li Guojie transferred it to the Business Corporation. Later, after Chen Fumu left office, the Ministry of Communications discovered the situation in November of the same year and ordered the Shanghai Municipal Government to hand over Li Guojie to the prosecutor of the Shanghai District Court for investigation and prosecution.

(Reasoning) The crime of breach of trust under Article 366 of the Criminal Code requires the intention to obtain illegal benefits for oneself or a third party, or the intention to cause illegal harm to the principal. In this case, the loan agreements signed by the appellant with the American China Business Corporation on September 5th and 6th, 1932, in the name of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, stipulated that the building loan portion would use the land owned by the company along the Fuzhou Road waterfront and Sichuan Road in Shanghai as collateral, borrowing Shanghai taels 10 million, and the dock loan portion would use the Shanghai Zhongbei, Huanan, and Xinwu docks owned by the company as collateral, borrowing Shanghai taels 10 million, both at 85% of face value, with a commission of 2%, an annual interest rate of 9%, and a term of 20 years. During the term or before the secured loan was repaid, if the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company wished to sell all or part of the mortgaged property, the Business Corporation had the preemptive right to purchase the mortgaged property or part of it. If it could not fulfill the agreement as scheduled, the Business Corporation had the right to sell the mortgaged property without the consent of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Regardless of any disputes, impartial persons had to be hired to determine them according to current American law. The memorandum of understanding for the purchase of ships on credit also stipulated that 30 ships would be purchased by the Dalae Shipping Company on behalf of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company for use in the company's operations on the Yangtze River and in the northern and southern oceans. Before the price of the ships was paid in full, all the ships would be registered in the United States and fly the American flag. The national government would be exempt from any legal restrictions on foreign merchant ships operating along the Yangtze River and coastal areas of China. These terms were indeed excessive. If they were fully implemented, the assets and navigation rights of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company would be damaged. However, the investigation of the agreement and the testimony of the manager of the Business Corporation, Lu Deli, revealed that the 85% discount was related to the issuance of bonds, and the 2.5% commission was solely received by the lender, which was in line with the financial ministry's response and the usual practice of borrowing foreign debt approved by the court. The appellant did not have the intention to obtain illegal benefits for himself or a third party. His intention, as stated in his report to the Vice Minister of Communications and Supervisor of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, was to repay old debts, redeem mortgaged assets, add ships, build docks, and expand business. There was no evidence to show that his intention was to cause illegal harm to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Therefore, his signing of the agreements, regardless of whether they violated his duties, did not meet the essential elements of the aforementioned crime. The damage to others mentioned in that provision refers to specific facts. Although the agreements signed by the appellant with the China Business Corporation were harsh, if the reorganization could be implemented and the loan repaid on time, the damage would not occur. It could be said that there was a risk of damage, but not that damage was caused. Therefore, the original trial's determination that the appellant signed the agreements to harm the assets and navigation rights of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and convicted him of the crime of attempted commission under Article 266, Paragraph 1 and Article 140 of the Criminal Code was incorrect. The appellant's claim that the original judgment was improper is not without merit. As for the 700,000 taels paid by the appellant to the China Business Corporation on September 23, 1932, and handed over to Huang Jusu, the representative of Chen Fumu, the Vice Minister of Communications and Supervisor of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, not only did the appellant confess clearly, but the original prosecutor and this court also investigated the Business Corporation and found ten checks from the Maccalee Bank, Nos. 5115 to 5124, and one check from the HSBC, No. 6815414, each worth taels 10,000, and two checks, Nos. 681522 and 681523, and one check from the Citibank, No. D4859, each worth foreign 71,736.01 yuan, equivalent to taels 50,000 at a rate of 0.0697, all under the names of Chen Shaode, Chen Zeqing, Wei Junhong, Wei Zhenhong, Huang Weiru, Huang Zhongde, Huang Zhengde, Huang Zhide, Feng Ruiyi, Feng Shuyan, and deposited in the Zhongfu, Jin Cheng, Shanghai, and China banks, and the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, which were subsequently withdrawn one after another, leaving only a small balance. The deposit dates were September 24th, 26th, 27th, and 29th, coinciding with the date of payment. The addresses of the depositors, such as 5 Zhaofeng Village, according to the gatekeeper Zhang, used to be the Huang Mansion, and 28 Meiliyuan, Daxi Road, according to Qu Shu and Yao Dekui, who lived in the alleyway, Chen Fumu had lived there before and moved away in November 1932. Furthermore, the appellant stated that he had heard that Chen Fumu's wife was a Wei, and Huang Jusu's wife was a Feng, so the depositors Chen Shaode, Chen Zeqing, Wei Junhong, Wei Zhenhong, Huang Weiru, Huang Zhongde, Huang Zhengde, Huang Zhide, Feng Ruiyi, Feng Shuyan were pseudonyms of Chen Fumu and his wife Huang Jusu. It can be inferred that the appellant's statement that he handed over 700,000 taels to Huang Jusu, the representative of Chen Fumu, is credible. Although the appellant stated that he handed over the money to the supervisor for safekeeping, and the supervisor said that the agreement stipulated that the money would only be paid when the bonds were issued, and that if the Business Corporation did not issue the bonds, they would be affected, and the supervisor was very worried and asked to negotiate with him to pay this amount first as a guarantee of credit, so it was called an advance payment. Supervisor Chen Fumu was the head of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and the manager was under him. He had to keep the money, and the general manager had no power to say no. However, in his report to the Ministry of Communications on November 15, 1932, the appellant stated that the money was demanded by Chen Fumu and handed over to Chen Fumu, and that he swore to God that he had not taken a single cent. During the prosecutor's investigation, the appellant stated that the building loan was signed on September 5th, and the dock contract and the purchase of ships on credit were signed on September 6th. Around September 3rd, the supervisor approved the signing. After the signing, he officially submitted a request to the supervisor's office to affix the official seal, but the supervisor withheld the contract and refused to release it. At the same time, he asked someone to express the need to raise some money, but he refused to say what it was for. When the creditors urged him to sign the contract because they did not know about this situation, he had no choice but to ask the company to advance a batch of money. The foreign manager understood the situation in China very well and advanced the money. When asked when the contract was handed down, he replied that he handed over the money and the contract was handed over at the same time. When asked if the check was registered, he replied that it was not registered, and he demanded that it not be registered. When asked if he had any proof of handing over the money, he replied that he had no proof. When asked why he gave it to him without proof, he replied that it was not appropriate to ask for proof at that time. When asked if he was not afraid of breaking the law by giving Chen Fumu 700,000 taels, he replied that he was really afraid of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company closing down, so he did it. Because the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company had ships and docks, there was a chance for revival. His giving Chen Fumu 700,000 taels was also an intention to achieve great things by sacrificing small expenses. When asked how he would make up for this batch of money in the future, he replied that he would gradually make up for it after the business improved. He described the situation in which Chen Fumu demanded the money and he paid it in detail. Chen Fumu did not give the appellant any receipt, and the appellant did not use any official documents to explain the money, nor did he record it in any books. Therefore, it was clear that the money was not handed over to Chen Fumu for safekeeping. Although the appellant argued that the original report was not a voluntary statement, and his confession during the investigation was not his original intention, and that the receipt of the money could not be recorded in the ordinary accounting books of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company according to the contract, and that the general manager could not resist the supervisor's right to hand over the money without a receipt, he did not provide any concrete evidence to support his defense. Therefore, the appellant's claim that he handed over a bribe at the request of supervisor Chen Fumu is undoubtedly true. However, the appellant paid 700,000 taels to the Business Corporation as an advance payment for the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, handed it over to Chen Fumu without recording it in any books, and promised to make it up gradually when the business improved. This clearly shows an intention to illegally possess public property for a third party, which constitutes the crime of embezzlement of public property under Article 357, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code. This crime is connected to the crime of giving bribes. According to Article 74 of the Criminal Code, the more serious crime should be punished. However, the original trial failed to consider this embezzlement, which was a mistake. Article 129, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Code, which prescribes a breach of duty, refers to failing to do what one should do. Chen Fumu, as the supervisor of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, was within his authority to stipulate and abolish contracts in accordance with Article 5, Paragraph 2 of the regulations of the supervisor's office of the company. The appellant, in giving Chen Fumu 700,000 taels when he requested bribes at the time of affixing the seal to the loan agreement, only gave a bribe to a public official for an act within the scope of his duties, which constituted the crime of Article 128, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Code. The original trial incorrectly convicted him of the crime of Article 129, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Code. Furthermore, Article 129 (Paragraph 4 provides for confiscation or recovery only for crimes under Paragraphs 1 and 2 of the same article. The original trial found the appellant guilty of a crime under Paragraph 3 and ordered the confiscation of the 700,000 taels or the recovery if it was lost, which was not only without legal basis but also violated the provisions of the second half of Article 12 of the Criminal Code, and its legal interpretation was also wrong. Furthermore, Article 30, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Code, "the person with the right to claim" refers to a crime that is prosecuted only upon complaint. Bribery is not a crime that is prosecuted only upon complaint. The Minister of Communications is not the victim or the complainant. The appellant's report of handing over the money to Chen Fumu did not intend to have the case adjudicated by the competent public official and did not meet the conditions for surrendering under that article. The original trial incorrectly applied that article to reduce the sentence by one-half, which was also inappropriate. The appellant's argument denying the crime, but attempting to exonerate himself, is not justified. However, the original judgment was improper in this respect and should be revoked and revised. Based on the above considerations, in accordance with Article 315, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Procedure Law, Article 357, Paragraph 1, Article 120, Paragraph 2, Article 74, Article 362, Article 57, Paragraph 5, Article 56, Article 64 of the Criminal Code, and Articles 379 and 316 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the judgment is as stated in the main text. This case was executed by the prosecutor of this court, Zan Fen. The appellate court in this case is the Supreme Court. If the parties do not agree with this judgment, they should file an appeal to this court within ten days from the day after the delivery of the judgment, stating the reasons for the disagreement in writing. June 5, 1933, First Criminal Division of the Jiangsu High Court, Presiding Judge Lin Zhezhang, Judge Si Wen, Judge Fang Wen.

Robot Traffic Light

Satisfactory Performance in Trials

Incorporates Various Principles

The "China Press" reports that a model of a robot traffic controller has arrived in Shanghai. It was demonstrated to the police authorities of both concessions, and its performance was deemed highly satisfactory. It is said that the managers and merchants are now planning to take it to Japan for demonstrations. The robot incorporates all the principles used in the 17-route traffic system of Trafalgar Square and is built to the same size as the famous London robot. The electromagnetic principles used in its electrical design are the same as those used in automatic telephones. When in use, it is first necessary to study the traffic conditions at the intersection, dividing the day into several time periods and counting the number of vehicles traveling in each direction per minute during each period. Then, the proportion of time for east-west traffic and north-south traffic is determined. This ratio is then set on the robot's timer table. The robot can then accurately switch the red and green lights during that period. In addition, rubber mechanisms are installed at each intersection. If there is no north-south traffic during the north-south traffic time, but there is east-west traffic, the vehicle passing over this rubber mechanism will cause the robot to temporarily switch the direction of the traffic lights for four seconds so that the vehicle can proceed immediately without having to wait for the scheduled traffic time. This combination of timed operation and adaptation to actual traffic is a new invention of the robot and has never been seen before.

Summary of the Jiangxi Nanchang Labor Relief Project of the Jisheng Society

The Shanghai Chinese Jisheng Society's labor relief project for repairing the Guangfeng Dike in the western district of Nanchang County, Jiangxi Province, publicly appointed Mr. Li Yunmen as the director, along with relief workers Gu Yabin, Sun Xixian, and others. On February 10th of this year, they took the relief funds and traveled by boat to Jiangxi, as reported in a previous issue. According to Mr. Li Yunmen's report upon his return to Shanghai, construction began on February 26th. A section of the Guangfeng Dike was repaired, approximately 12-13 feet high, with a base width ranging from 30-40 feet and a surface width of 10 feet, totaling over 32,600 cubic feet of work. Three culverts were also built. A wooden bridge was built in Yushe Town, 96 feet long, 12 feet wide, and 28 feet high. All projects have been completed. However, due to excessive rainfall this year, the water level was too low to start construction on the large water gate. It has not yet been completed and cannot be proceeded with until the water recedes. The dike and bridge project used more than 23,000 yuan in relief funds, including 6,500 yuan donated by the China and Foreign Relief Association and 1,500 yuan donated by the Moral Society. If the gate project is completed, there will still be a shortage of 2,300 yuan. No sooner was the construction of the dam and bridge completed than the Han and Yangtze Rivers flooded, and the provinces of Hangzhou and Hubei suffered major disasters. Jiangxi Province, being downstream of the Yangtze River, is also in imminent danger. It is hoped that the weather will clear up soon so that the situation can be turned from danger to safety. Recently, Mr. Huang Wenzhi, a gentry from Jiangxi Province, came to the association to report that thanks to the early completion of the project, there would have been cause for great concern due to the heavy rains. The unfinished relief work still needs to be continued. The old relief work has not been completed, and new relief work is needed. Now that there has been continuous flooding, the rural life in China depends entirely on the dikes, so that the people can be safe. Patriotic people and charitable people are requested to pay attention to this matter.

Eighteen Kidnappers Handed Over to the Second Special District Court

Wang Delin, the young son (nine years old) of Wang Fusun, a famous architect from Ningbo, residing at 2 Dafeng Lane, Huanlong Road in the French Concession, was suddenly kidnapped by kidnappers at 5:00 AM on December 28th of last year. They demanded a ransom of 400,000 yuan. Negotiations failed, and it was not until April of this year that the police of the Public Concession uncovered the location where he was being held, rescued the hostage, and returned him to his family. The kidnappers, Wang Yuanwei, Zhang Xiaomao, Yao Sheng, Qian Ziming, Cai Xilin, Chen Guoqian, Wu Yesong, Qian Changmei, Chen Abing, Madam He Ma, Madam Shi Yu, Madam Chen Qiu, Madam Shen Ma, Madam Chen Zhang, Madam Zhang Wang, Wu Xiangfeng, Shen Qian, Chen Zhang, and 18 men and women, mostly from Shaoxing, were arrested. Because the kidnappers were also found to have committed kidnapping cases in the Public Concession, they were first handed over to the First Special District Court for trial. Wang Yuanwei was sentenced to life imprisonment, Zhang Xiaomao to ten and a half years, and Yao Sheng to nine and a half years. The remaining people were sentenced according to the severity of their crimes. Those who were not involved were declared innocent. The French police recently asked the Second Special District Court to prepare a document. Jin Jiulin, an inspector from the Special Agency, along with detectives Zhang Ziying, Zhou Yaoting, Zhou Bingcheng, and bailiffs Cai Jinzhang and Qin Youyu, went to the First Special District Court to transfer Wang and 17 other men and women to the French police. Yesterday, they were handed over to the Criminal Division 1 of the Second Special District Court. Judge Cai Changnian conducted the preliminary hearing. Lawyer Gu Shouxi of the police station stated the details of the case, stating that the 18 defendants were transferred from the First Special District Court of the Public Concession. The defendants confessed that they were involved in the kidnapping case of Wang Delin, the son of Wang Fusun, at 2 Dafeng Lane, Huanlong Road, on December 28th of last year. The police station had not yet completed the investigation. Due to the large number of people, the investigation would take time. He requested a postponement of three weeks for a detailed investigation. If any defendants were found not to be involved, the police station could release them first and return them to the First Special District Court. The court reviewed the report and questioned the defendants one by one. The hearing was postponed to 9:00 AM on July 13th. Those who were found to be not suspicious during the period would be sent for trial in advance to facilitate their release. The 18 defendants were detained.

Jiangxi Provincial Government Announces the State of Production Decline 64

(Nanchang) The Provincial Government's Economic Council announced that the decline in production is alarming: (1) The annual rice production is approximately 6.6 million dan. Exports in 1928 were worth 17 million yuan, which decreased to 2 million yuan in 1931. This year, there are no exports. (2) During the heyday of Jingdezhen porcelain production, there were more than 500 kilns. In 1928, there were more than 100 kilns. This year, there are only dozens of kilns, many of which are not firing. (3) Tobacco once ranked third in the country, with an annual output of 330,000 dan. In 1931, exports were only 52,000 dan, ranking fifth. (4) The annual tea production is approximately 500,000 dan, with exports of over 320,000 dan. In 1931, exports were only 100,000 dan. (5) Annual timber exports were approximately 16 million cubic feet. Recently, timber in the Gan River has become almost exhausted. (6) Southern Jiangxi's tin ore accounts for 16% of the world's total. Recently, it has been severely reduced. Other items such as tung oil and paper have also changed from large-scale exports to imports. Last year, imports of cigarettes amounted to 4.47 million customs taels, second only to cotton textiles. The consumption expenditure in two years could complete the main roads of the province. (23rd Special Dispatch)
