Shanghai City First, Second, Third Districts

[District Education Association General Meeting]

△ The First District Changed to a Lecture Meeting Due to Insufficient Numbers

△ Wang Diyan and Four Others Elected as Secretaries in the Second District

△ Tang Liqing and Four Others Elected as Secretaries in the Third District

The terms of office for the secretaries of the district education associations in the city have expired after one year, and they have been re-elected one after another. It is learned that the education associations in the first, second, and third districts held general meetings of members yesterday afternoon. Except for the First District Education Association, which changed to a lecture meeting due to insufficient members attending according to legal requirements, the secretaries of the Second and Third Districts have been elected. Details are as follows:

First District 81

The First District Education Association held its third general meeting of members at Jingye Middle School at 1:00 p.m. yesterday. Cao Peizi, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Zheng Hongnian, representative of the Municipal Education Association, and members Yang Jingyi, Shi Renzheng, Zhang Lichun, Chen Rongfa, and others, totaling 262 people, were present. The presidium consisted of Tao Guangchuan, Zhao Luqing, and Zhang Yongchun. The recorder was Jiang Luolin. First, Chairman Tao Guangchuan reported that there are a total of more than 700 members in the district, but the number of attendees today is insufficient to meet the legal requirements, so it will be changed to a lecture meeting. Next, Wang Yunwu gave a lecture, stating that teachers bear the responsibility of educating young people and have a great impact on society, especially primary and secondary school teachers who educate children, which has an even greater impact. Rousseau said that educating children should allow for the development of their personality. This statement may be appropriate in countries that are already on track, but it is not suitable for the morbid state of China. Chinese teachers are like doctors, and they should find the shortcomings of the national character and use education to correct them. The biggest common disease of the Chinese people is the lack of communication, such as between mouth and heart, hand and chest, spirit and matter, and individual and society. Communication is lacking everywhere, especially among educated people. Therefore, those who run education in our country must not allow children to develop their personality at random, but must use the methods of doctors to treat this disease. There are many ways to treat the disease, but none are as effective as primary and secondary school teachers who guide them everywhere in practical education. Finally, Zheng Hongnian gave a speech, the content of which is omitted. The meeting then adjourned.

Second District 82

The Second District Education Association held a general meeting of members at Tangjia Lane Primary School at 2:00 p.m. yesterday. Du Gang, Wu Xiu, Lu Zhaiqian, Mao Yun, and others, as well as Cao Peizi, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Ding Shoutang, representative of the Municipal Education Bureau, Ma Jiazhen, representative of the Municipal Education Association, and guest Lu Jizeng, totaling more than 70 people, were present. The presidium consisted of Wang Dingcheng, Du Gang, and Cai Hongtian. The recorder was Zhang Yunchi, and the master of ceremonies was Zhang Shuting. After the ceremony, Chairman Wang Dingcheng gave a report. Cao Peizi of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Ding Shoutang of the Municipal Education Bureau, and Ma Jiazhen of the Municipal Education Association gave instructions. Finally, Lu Jizeng gave a speech. Then, the secretaries were elected. Wang Diyan, Wang Dingcheng, Shen Xibin, Lu Zhaiqian, and Song Bingqin were elected as secretaries. Xu Yuma and Gu Xubing were elected as alternate secretaries. The newly elected secretaries took office and were sworn in under the supervision of Cao Peizi of the Municipal Party Headquarters. Finally, proposals were discussed: (1) Whether the general meeting should issue a declaration; (2) Request the Municipal Education Bureau to add municipal elementary schools in the district to benefit school-age children; (3) Organize community schools to promote education; (4) Request the Municipal Education Bureau to forward a letter to the Municipal Government requesting that the French Concession provide financial assistance equal to 20% of its total annual income to private Chinese schools in the French Concession before the right to education in the concession is returned to China; (5) Request the Municipal Education Bureau to forward a request to the Municipal Government to take back the right to education in the concession; (6) Request the Education Bureau to forward a request to the Ministry of Education to revoke the restriction on universities recruiting liberal arts students; (7) Whether members of the district should hold gatherings to connect with each other. All of the above cases were handed over to the secretariat for handling. The meeting then adjourned.

Third District 83

The Third District Education Association held a general meeting of members at Shuji Primary School at 2:00 p.m. yesterday. Huang Yangren, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Cheng Guoxiang, representative of the Municipal Education Bureau, Chen Jicheng, representative of the Municipal Education Association, Gu Fuwu of the Third District Party Headquarters, and members Tang Liqing, Zhou Darong, and Chen Pinqi, totaling more than 180 people, were present. The presidium consisted of Tang Liqing, Xu Shushen, and Yang Zhenzhong. The master of ceremonies was Ai Rong, and the recorder was Zhu Xiaolin. After the ceremony, Chairman Xu Shushen gave an opening speech, and Tang Liqing reported on the work of the first secretariat. Then, representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Municipal Education Bureau, the Municipal Education Association, and the Third District Party Headquarters gave speeches. Finally, the election was held. Tang Liqing, Xu Huimin, Yan Youren, Xu Peixing, and Yang Zhenzhong were elected as secretaries. The meeting adjourned after the election.

Municipal Education Bureau Handles the Pudong Student Strike 84

▲ If Principal Wu is Unable to Take Responsibility in Fact ▲ An Order for the Board of Directors to Appoint a New Principal

(Shanghai News Agency) A minor dispute occurred at the Private Pudong Middle School in this city due to student dissatisfaction with the measures of Principal Wu and one or two faculty members. After receiving the report, the Municipal Education Bureau immediately sent personnel to investigate. At the same time, fearing that bad elements would take the opportunity to stir up trouble, it notified the Municipal Public Security Bureau to instruct the Pudong Public Security Third District Branch to send police to pay attention at any time to prevent accidents. In order to prevent the expansion of the dispute, in addition to ordering the school's board of directors to quickly decide on a proper solution, it also persuaded the students to attend classes with peace of mind and wait for a thorough investigation. Since then, the students have continued to attend classes, and all have fully participated in the secondary school graduation joint exam. However, it is reported that the principal has not been to school recently, resulting in no one responsible for the school and the school administration almost completely suspended. The Education Bureau learned that at this time, when the semester is about to end, it is deeply concerned that this will affect student learning and the school's facilities for the next year. It has urged the school's board of directors to convene a meeting as soon as possible to discuss a solution. If it is deemed that Principal Wu is in fact unable to take responsibility, a new principal should be selected to take over as soon as possible to rectify the situation. If the board of directors cannot convene or the meeting is adjourned, the chairman of the board of directors is responsible for submitting a reorganization plan to the Education Bureau for approval to facilitate rectification. It is expected that this matter will be completely resolved soon.

A Record of the Third Day of the College Guidance Movement Week 85

▲Yesterday was Middle School Day: Today is Women's School Day

Yesterday was the Middle School Day of the College Guidance Movement Week organized by the Vocational Education Society of China's Vocational Guidance Institute. Despite continuous rain, the weather suddenly cleared up in the morning, and the number of visitors and attendees increased several times. The details are recorded below:

▲Lecture Situation

At 9:00 AM, Mr. Yang Weiyu and Mr. Pan Yangyao presided over the opening ceremony and gave introductory speeches. They were followed by Mr. Tao Baichuan, Mr. Ni Wenya, and Mr. Li Zongwen who gave successive speeches. In the afternoon, Mr. Zheng Xigu and Mr. Chen Binhe gave speeches. (The lecture notes recorded by the Bingxun Speed ​​Writing Agency, by Mr. Liu Dihua.)

▲Attendees

Yesterday's attendees and visitors included Cai Wuji, Zhang Wei, Xu Wancheng, Huang Jingwan, and students from Wuben, Shanghai Women's Supplementary School, Tonghui, Bide, Tang Tao, Hua Long, Guoben, Henan Vocational School, as well as students from various municipal primary and secondary schools, totaling six to seven hundred people in the morning and afternoon.

▲Popularity of the College Guidance

The "College Guidance" book compiled and printed by the institute to guide young people in their higher education has been praised by attendees in recent days as an excellent book that is both affordable and of high quality. Many people have bought and read it, with almost everyone having a copy in hand.

▲Increased Exhibits

In addition to the books sent by Commercial Press, Zhonghua Book Company, World Book Company, Datong Book Company, Shanghai College, Sanlin Vocational School, Huahua Middle School, and Shanghai Women's Supplementary School, the number of books displayed at the association have increased. In recent days, there have also been textbooks and reference books from Qinfen Bookstore, Life Bookstore, Beixin Bookstore, and Women's Bookstore, various maps from the Shanghai Geographical Society, as well as charts from Peking Yanjing University, Xiamen University, Shanghai Women's University, and a variety of school regulations from other schools. The maps of various university departments, university locations, distribution maps, and comparison tables of tuition fees drawn by the institute were especially noticed by young people seeking higher education.

▲Bright Light Company Gifts Fans

The Bright Light Thermos Company donated specially made exquisite paper fans to be distributed on the spot, citing the large number of attendees in recent days and the hot weather.

▲Mr. Tao's Speech, entitled "Opportunities for Poor Students to Study," stated briefly that the average income for a man trying to find a job in Shanghai is less than 50 yuan. If a family has five members, the monthly expenditure is at least 70 or 80 yuan. Under such circumstances, it is not easy to send children to study. Therefore, (1) poor children have very few opportunities to receive education at this time. (2) If we can barely afford to go to school, we should also consider whether our mothers can afford it. Now, let me introduce you to an economical and reliable school, which is Jingye Middle School. The total cost per semester is only 60 yuan. Poor students with excellent grades can also get free tuition. As for purchasing books, we can combine several students to pool funds for joint reading, which is much more economical, etc.

▲Mr. Ni's Speech, entitled "How to Receive Secondary Education," stated briefly: (1) Before entering middle school, you must recognize what secondary education is and pay attention to: 1. What is your personal intelligence like? 2. Pay attention to the family's financial situation. 3. What is the current trend? (2) What to do after entering middle school: 1. Pay attention to physical and mental cultivation. 2. All subjects must be developed evenly. 3. Do not give up the opportunity to study, such as listening to lectures by famous people or talking with teachers, etc.

▲Mr. Li's speech briefly stated: (1) Choose your personal interests. (2) Determine your aspirations for studying. (3) Assess your abilities. (4) Study schools of the same nature that you want to enter: 1. Observe and investigate the history of the school. 2. Whether the equipment is perfect. 3. Whether the fees are within your financial ability. 4. What are the career prospects of each graduating class and whether they can gain social trust. 5. Whether the school's faculty and staff are responsible, enthusiastic about education, and seek happiness for students. 6. Whether the school's atmosphere and reputation are good. (5) Only by entering a good school can you get good results, etc.

▲Mr. Zheng's speech briefly stated that in the current situation in China, it is a declining and unorganized spirit of independent countries. Education is not in line with the needs of society. The talents that emerge are of no help to the country. Therefore, when talking about young people receiving secondary education, it is necessary to say three points: (1) Cultivate a strong physique and a spirit of enduring hardship. (2) Break the concept of scholar-officials and practice manual and mental labor to support oneself. (3) Pay special attention to applied science to cultivate and increase production capacity, etc.

▲Mr. Chen's speech briefly stated that among the more than 200,000 middle school students in China, they account for 1/1700th of the country's population, that is, only one middle school student out of more than 1,700 people has the opportunity to be a middle school student. Although this is so good, you must pay attention to: (1) Under the severe situation of internal and external troubles in China, each middle school student bears the responsibility of more than 1,700 people to save the endangered nation. (2) Have the hard work and endurance to see the people of Russia, you can know that they are able to work hard and endure to achieve the success of the three-year plan. (3) Take a skeptical attitude, if there are lessons that you don't understand, you must thoroughly understand them clearly, and never repeat what others say. This is the law of middle school students, etc.

▲Tomorrow is Women's School Day

Today is Women's School Day, which is also the last chance. At 9:00 AM, Ms. Yang Qianzhen, Principal of the Chinese and Western Girls' School, Mr. Lu Guiliang, and Ms. Shen Shijing, Director of Academic Affairs of Weiji Primary School, will give speeches. At 4:00 PM, Ms. Wang Xiaoying, Principal of Wuben Girls' School, and Ms. Huang Shaolan, Principal of Bowen Girls' School, will give speeches. Students from various schools can go to listen, etc.

Phonetic Competition to be Held Tomorrow 87

▲Registration still available this morning

The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association is holding phonetic symbol competitions across the country, as reported in this newspaper. Now, the Shanghai side has decided to hold it at Shuji Primary School in Tianhou Palace, starting at 8:00 AM tomorrow. The competition rules of the association are listed below: (1) This competition is limited to second-year students of Shanghai Municipal Primary Schools (each school sends two students). (2) The standard of this competition is based on accuracy and speed. (3) The competition items are divided into two types: phonetic notation and phonetic transcription of Chinese characters. (4) The competition time is limited to 30 minutes (those who finish before the time limit can raise their right hand to compete). (5) Contestants should pay attention to the following matters: 1. Enter the seat according to the competition certificate number and do not change it arbitrarily. 2. In addition to stationery such as pencils and erasers, do not bring other items. 3. Do not leave your seat during the competition. (6) During the competition, three kinds of commands will be issued: 1. Prepare (when the contestants hear the word "Prepare," they will immediately take their right hand and hold the pencil, and immediately raise their right hand when the word "Prepare" is issued). 2. Compete (when the contestants hear the "Competition" command, they will immediately write the phonetic notation or translate). 3. Stop (when the contestants hear the "Stop" command, no matter whether they have finished writing or not, they will immediately raise their right hand, and after the test paper is collected, they can put down their right hand). (7) The judging score is calculated as a percentage. Phonetic notation of Chinese characters and phonetic translation of Chinese characters each account for 50 points, totaling 100 points. One point will be deducted for each wrong character or spelling. The ranking will be determined by the total score. (8) The judging results will be broadcast on Shanghai Radio at 4:00 PM on June 25, and will be published in various newspapers on June 26. (9) Prizes will be awarded at Shuji Primary School, Tianhou Palace Bridge at 2:00 PM on June 2. (10) Visitors should pay attention to the following matters: 1. Do not talk. 2. Do not move around. 3. Do not smoke. It is also heard that the Fuzhou side, organized by Zhang Yongrong, the phonetic committee member of the association, is scheduled to be held at Fuzhou No. 1 Primary School, Dongjie, Fuzhou City on July 4.

Soochow Law School Changes Organization 93

▲Following the Ministry of Education's Educational System Regulations

▲Four Years of University, Three Years of Graduate School

The academic system of the Law School of Soochow University in Shanghai is five years of university and two years of graduate school, which is different from ordinary universities. Now, in order to comply with the regulations of the university system of the Ministry of Education and to improve the level of admission, the school has decided to change the organization through the school affairs meeting. The university is set for four years, and the graduate school is for three years. The first year of university is dedicated to social sciences, and the next three years are for law. The graduate school will explore the jurisprudence of the United Kingdom, the United States, and various countries on the mainland. Those with one year of university education can be inserted into the second grade for study. Graduates of law universities recognized by the school who have been awarded a Bachelor of Laws degree can apply to the graduate school as researchers. The method of this change in organization has been submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval and filing, and will be implemented in the next semester.

How to Protect Your Radio During the Rainy Season 102

— He Dazhi

(1) Reasons why radios are easily damaged during the rainy season

All electrical appliances are most susceptible to dampness. And the radio's sensitivity is very acute, so the impact of dampness on the radio is significant, so the radio is most vulnerable during the rainy season. When the radio is wet, because water is a conductor, the current can escape through moisture (this phenomenon is called leakage). Or the wire is broken due to corrosion caused by moisture, resulting in a variety of problems.

(2) Radio's own failures

When the radio is working, if you touch the coil with your hand, the sensitivity of the radio will immediately decrease. If the regenerative force is not fully enhanced, it will be completely silent. The same result is obtained by touching the grid leak or grid capacitor or the grid wire of the high-frequency amplifier tube. That is, when the coil or grid wire is damp, it also reduces the sensitivity, weakens the regenerative force, and deteriorates the selectivity.

Secondly, after the low-frequency transformer is dampened, the volume is reduced, and the winding is easily broken. This type of failure is the second most common cause of radio damage. (Vacuum tube failure is the most common cause of radio damage.) After the power transformer is dampened, the insulation of each part becomes poor, which reduces the volume and generates extremely large AC noise (Hum).

Therefore, the location of the radio must be in a place with good air circulation, dryness, and little dust (after the dust adheres, the dust easily absorbs moisture). During the rainy season, on sunny days, the radio must be moved to the window for ventilation and wipe off the dust.

When purchasing a radio, you must choose a fully enclosed case with components and wiring hidden inside the case, so that the chance of dust and moisture intrusion is less harmful.

(3) Loudspeaker failure

This type of failure is the same as that of a low-frequency transformer, and the internal winding is easily broken. In addition, the poor wiring causes the current flowing into the loudspeaker coil to leak, which reduces the volume. When this type of failure occurs, the wires can be replaced with new ones.

Figure 1 Poorly insulated wire

Symbol representation

Radio current

Leakage current

(4) Antenna failure When insulators and supports are damp, more radio waves leak to the ground (as shown in Figure 2), which causes the sensitivity to become dull, the regenerative force to be weak, and the selectivity to be poor. However, the insulators cannot be wiped clean one by one, so it is better to use two insulators connected together.

Figure 2

Dotted line shown

Is due to insulation

Poor body and

Leakage current

Indoor lead-in wires are mostly covered wires, so they should not be nailed to walls that are easily damp, but to wooden pillars or wooden beams.

(5) Battery When the protruding surface or sides of the battery poles are damp, the current leaks and the battery consumption increases. (As shown in Figure 3) If the battery placed in the radio case has this phenomenon and comes into contact with other circuits, it can even make the radio silent.

Therefore, the battery should be placed in a dry and well-ventilated place like the radio, and it should be wiped with a cloth from time to time to remove dust. If A and B batteries are storage batteries, special attention should be paid to them.

(6) Precautions during thunderstorms

There are often thunderstorms during the rainy season, which increases the noise of the radio and even disrupts the reception. At this time, of course, the antenna switch must be turned down to connect it to the ground wire. For AC radios, the power plug must also be unplugged.

It is currently the rainy season, and anyone with a radio should take extra care to protect it to avoid unexpected losses. (The end) (Translated and excerpted from "Wireless Telephone")

Common Sense for Using Radios in Summer 103

— Cheng Quan

(1) The entire radio should be placed in a dry place to prevent mold from entering and damaging the radio. (2) Place several packages of quicklime inside the radio to absorb moisture. (3) Install lightning protection equipment in the antenna circuit. Or connect the sky and ground lines during thunderstorms to avoid accidents. (4) If the AC radio is used for too long. The fuselage heats up. Then rest for a few minutes before turning it on again. Or in the primary power supply inlet line. Directly connect a light bulb. (Watts are equal to the radio. The bulb is dimly red). Then even if it is used for a long time. It will not heat up.

(5) When the A, B, and C batteries of the DC radio are not in use. Be sure to remove the lead wires from the machine to avoid leakage from the wooden box. (6) For long and short wave radios that use plug-in coils. The coil must be placed in the driest place. Otherwise it is very easy to fail. (7) The radio distance is not far. The volume and sound quality deteriorate. This is affected by the climate. Do not dismantle and repair it rashly.

The Resurrection Method of Dry Batteries 104

— Jing

The use of electricity and the progress of the world are always directly proportional. The more advanced the world is, the wider the use of electricity becomes. Therefore, in recent years, the use of electricity has been increasing day by day. Dry batteries are one example. For example, flashlights, small radios, and other machines that require less electricity use them. Since the prevalence of radios, the sales of dry batteries have flourished accordingly. Although alternating current can be used to replace dry batteries, it always feels a bit troublesome from a procedural and economic point of view, not to mention that today's one or two tube machines all use dry batteries? But there is one thing that is very regrettable, that is, the power of dry batteries is limited. Once they are used up, they are useless. You can only buy new ones. Isn't this very uneconomical? Now there is a way to make the used dry batteries repeat their electricity. Now I will write this method below and introduce it to readers, hoping that they will use it more and try to save money as much as possible. Take saltpeter (Ammoniachloride) and dissolve it in a bowl (it doesn't have to be a bowl, just something made of glass or clay) of warm water to make a saturated solution (that is, pour saltpeter into the water, stir with a stick, wait until it is completely dissolved in the water, or completely disappeared, then add saltpeter again, stir again, until it can no longer be dissolved in the water). Then take the used dry battery whose shell is not damaged, and open a few small holes in its shell, and then put it in this solution. After putting it in for a few hours, take it out and it will have electricity. This method has been tried by me several times. Although the resurrected dry battery does not last as long as the new one when used (at least it has ten hours of electricity), it is much cheaper than buying a new one. Finally, I want to state that when placing it in the solution, you must not let the carbon rod in the middle touch the solution, otherwise it will not take effect. Note: Such resurrection is possible three times, but the power is reduced each time.

Small Experience

Two Methods for Winding Shortwave Coils 105

— Xiang

The plug-in coil of the shortwave radio is easy to loosen because it needs to be replaced frequently. To avoid this drawback, you only need to heat the wire next to the stove when winding it. After the wire is heated, it will expand by itself. Then, while it is hot, quickly wrap it on the rubber tube. After cooling, the wire shrinks. This coil is tightly wrapped around the rubber tube and is very firm and will not loosen for a long time. Wire hemp rope

Sometimes the coil needs to be wound with spacing (SpacingWinding), that is, each turn must be separated by an equal distance. This type of coil is quite difficult to wind. The easiest method is to wrap another hemp rope together with the wire. The thickness of the hemp rope depends on the distance required. After the winding is completed, remove the hemp rope and the wire will be very neat. (As shown in the picture)

Made of glass tube

Small Variable Capacitor 106

— Li Yuanqing

Paste a layer of semi-circular tin foil on the outside of the glass tube used to hold Western medicine, and then paste a layer of tin foil on a round piece of wood of considerable size in the same way. When using, insert the round wood into the glass tube, and then put the glass tube on the cork to form a small variable capacitor.

Elementary Introduction to Transmitters (Part 1) 107

— Huang Jiancun

▲..........

(1) Overview

Since transmitters differ in the method of generating oscillating current, they are divided into four types: spark type, arc type, generator type, and vacuum tube type. The advantages and disadvantages of these types will be described below. The spark type uses spark discharge to generate free oscillation in the oscillation circuit, and then transmits it to the antenna and emits it into space. This method was very popular in the wireless telegraph industry in the past, but because the radio waves it emits are so-called damped waves, containing a wide range of wavelengths, which interfere with other communications, the Third International Wireless Telegraph Conference held in Washington in 1927 stipulated that it should be prohibited from use from 1930. It can be asserted that this method will disappear by 1940. Before the invention of the vacuum tube, some people also tried to use the instantaneous quenching spark type with less damping rate for wireless telephone experiments, but because it has the disadvantages of noise caused by sparks and unclear sound, it has not been put into practical use. Although the arc type also belongs to the method of transmitting equal amplitude radio waves, the occurrence of electric arcs is prone to unstable states, and because it cannot transmit pure equal amplitude radio waves, the noise is more than other equal amplitude radio wave types, which also interferes with other communications, so it is still prohibited by international radio treaties, suffering the same fate as the spark type. This method has many noises, poor clarity, and is not suitable for short wavelengths, so it cannot be converted to wireless telephones. The generator type can transmit pure equal amplitude radio waves and is still popular in the long-wave radio telegraph industry. Since it can transmit pure equal amplitude radio waves, it is theoretically possible to use it for wireless telephones, but it is not easy to make it generate short waves like the current broadcast wave in terms of structure, and it also has the disadvantage of being difficult to adjust, so this method is still not applicable. The vacuum tube type can be said to be the darling of the current radio industry, and is very suitable for both wireless telegraph and wireless telephone. Wireless telephone only has today's prosperity due to the appearance of vacuum tubes. This is known to everyone. The reason why this method can occupy a dominant position is its characteristics: (1) It can transmit pure equal amplitude radio waves, (2) Wavelength and power can be used arbitrarily. (2) Clarity is excellent, etc. (To be continued)

Spring and Autumn

Disaster 108

— Baihe

It's really terrible. I don't know if China is destined to suffer disasters, or if "disaster" is particularly fond of China, which makes "great philanthropists" hold donation books all year round, looking for people to "help as they wish", and "great entertainers" tirelessly performing "to raise funds for relief." In short, China's "disaster star is flourishing" and "disaster luck is prosperous", which is undeniable.

"Airplanes dropping bombs" and "besieging cities and seizing territory" have created "disaster victims." A faction rises, and a B faction falls, "refreshing the officialdom," creating "disaster officials." The national power is declining, and diplomacy is humiliated, creating "disaster overseas Chinese." These are somewhat different from "dragons and floods breaking out", "locusts passing through the territory", and "not seeing a drop of rain for three years." I have no way to name them, so I name them "man-made disasters."

According to the news in the newspapers these days, the flood in Wuhan this year is inevitable to be "magnificent and grand." This is naturally a "natural disaster", and no one can blame anyone for "natural disasters", but they have to bite the bullet and appreciate the "taste of disaster."

In fact, Wuhan is only hit by floods every two years. When the water recedes, it will recover. There is no need to be alarmed. In Shaanxi and Gansu, it is so dry that crops cannot be planted. "Trading children for food" and "wild dogs eating people" are not uncommon. An eighteen-year-old girl doesn't even have pants to wear. That is considered a "particularly severe disaster."

These "disasters" are indeed scary, but they are still limited to one place. At most, they are like the "sixteen provinces hit by disaster" in the previous year. Now, except for the four northeastern provinces, there are still several provinces that have not been "hit by disaster." Only the "intellectual famine" that is prevalent throughout the country is qualified to "lead the group of disasters" and is considered the "leader in disaster."

China's disasters are more than just "three disasters and six difficulties." When Tang Seng went to the Western Paradise to seek scriptures, he did not encounter ninety-nine and eighty-one disasters, and they were still forcibly pieced together. If we calculate China's "natural disasters" and "man-made disasters", it may be more than this number. Tang Seng encountered eighty-one disasters, and he "completed his merits and became a righteous fruit." China has experienced so many "disasters", but it is still "a boundless sea of ​​suffering, and there is no shore to turn back." China, a country with many disasters and difficulties, still has not seen the disaster star recede, and the disasters are heavy, so some people say that the best way to relieve disasters is to summon high monks everywhere, start the Vajra Dharma Assembly, or recite scriptures and worship Buddha, in order to "invite heavenly blessings" and "eliminate disasters and bring blessings", so as to achieve "good weather and national prosperity and people's peace."

Fire 109

— Fu Yizhi

The cigarette paper shop on the ground floor of a single-family shop was like a smoke screen bomb, filling the entire space of the cigarette paper shop. Except for bursts of scorched air rushing straight into my nostrils, it was like falling into a five-mile thick fog, and I simply couldn't see myself clearly. If it hadn't been for the several Shandong fellows from the pancake shop next door waking me up, I would have unknowingly been buried in the fire pit, my soul would have vanished with the smoke, and my body would have been destroyed with the fire, without the pain of illness or the fear of death. How decisive! I was thinking like this. "Dangerous... not us..." From the thick smoke came one or two sentences with a hint of joy and a tone of claiming credit in the authentic Shandong accent. I knew that the fire had been extinguished by the Shandong fellows. "Amitabha, turning danger into safety"; the smoke has gradually thinned, and the Shandong fellows have gone to the pancake shop. Two girls, around ten years old, in the cigarette paper shop were standing there like wooden chickens. Their grandmother was taking a breath and slowly tidying up the ashes of the broken quilt. It is said that the fire was caused by this broken quilt falling on the mosquito incense. The little owner of the cigarette paper shop was sleeping upstairs with his new wife. From the time the fire started downstairs, to the fire was put out, he never came downstairs. He was a little panicked, letting his elderly mother and a pair of girls left by his ex-wife deal with this matter. The Bushidoists of the Fusang island country are no different from the god of fire. When this god of fire descends to the northwest corner, most of the indoor owners are still intoxicated in singing and dancing; on the night of January 28, the god of fire visited our inner room, but the owner was still in bed warming his sweet dream. Although there were a few people who put out the fire, and then someone burned incense and worshiped, they finally sent the god of fire away; not long ago. The embers in the northeast corner were rekindled, and spread to our north window, but, cutting off the fire │ no, only temporarily putting out the fire │, was also the dragon clock old lady borrowing the strength of the servant, didn't the little owner still sleep in bed talking about fire insurance? The Chinese are always so leisurely, what's wrong with the little owner of the small cigarette paper shop?

Ode to Candles 110

— Huo Xueming

This was my feeling one evening: the electric lights suddenly went out, and the streets at night were all plunged into darkness. My study could not distinguish all the objects. At this time, the eyes were almost the same as wax figures; they had no visual power, just like being trapped in a deep dark coal mine, where the safety light was suddenly blown out. You slipped out a spike of faint yellow red candlelight from the door seam of your neighborhood. Although it was a spike, it was brighter and more lovely than all the lights. A thing, when needed, is often unnoticed and thought to be useless; but it exerts extraordinary functions. So I quietly groped for the matches, struck a light, and searched for white candles on the dusty bookshelf. After spending five or six matches in a row, I found a white candle that had been gnawed by wild rats. Just this one burning and glued to the tea tray, the peach-shaped flame gave birth to awnings, spitting out light, illuminating the whole room. I felt that turning on the electric lights in the dimness of the day was far inferior to burning candles in the darkness of the night! The victory of the candle lies in its smallness in chewing fire!

If it is the Lunar New Year's Eve in the depth of winter, and snow is flying outside the window, in a mountain village; burning a red candle, leaning against the window to watch the plum blossoms and branches in the snow gradually getting fatter, due to the radiation of the candlelight, how beautiful is that scene! Moreover, there is a female poet standing next to her shoulder, both dizzy in the faint candlelight, silently looking at each other, followed by a smile, but very quiet; what kind of scene is that!

If you have talked about the Romance of the Three Kingdoms, you may think of a section in the twenty-fifth episode, saying that "Guan Gong surrendered to Cao Cao Cao wanted to disrupt the etiquette of his ministers, and made Guan Gong and his two sisters-in-law live in the same room. Guan Gong held a candle and stood outside the door, from night to dawn, without any fatigue." After understanding it, you will feel that a heroic general is vividly drawn in front of you, pressing his sword and cracking his eyes, staring angrily at the candlelight with that kind of awe-inspiring attitude!

At the moment when the candlelight flickered, I associated with the above two different realms. But I also noticed that the candletears were gradually falling, the candle heart was gradually shortening, and the remaining amount was also getting

less; I felt that burning like this would soon be extinguished, and I looked at my own shadow, and I was heartbroken. I wrote an old poem: "Looking at the curtain wave, the eye pattern, but pity the lonely shadow accompanied by dusk, wandering cloud temples are destroyed first, seeking light and the heart burns! :::" Really, those young people with poppy heads only understand fashionable ladies like flowers, only pursue abstract names, and Guangming makes a long and winding red dream. As a result, he only puts his own body, along with tears, in his own mystery-like aura, gradually shortens, gradually disappears, and gradually turns into green smoke. "Shedding tears for others until dawn"? However, after the dark night, it will always be dawn!

Untitled 111

— Chen Qibai

Who am I, wandering in the wind and dust? The remaining powder and rouge are all heartbreaking. Why do you need three million taels of gold? Just exchange your youth with your heart and blood. People suspect you are a teenager because of your demeanor. Stars have already dyed the temples with silk. Make a warm dream at the end of the world again. Perhaps it is a floating life that has not yet ended.

Depression 112

— Chen Qibai

Grand ambitions frustrated by hundreds of encounters. Duckweed roots and willow catkins take effort to arrange. Deep affection wants to tell the vast feeling. Bitter wine is poured in vain to relieve depression. It is better to escape Zen, life is a temporary residence. Finally need to insert lotus in death and bury it. The taste of great sorrow is thoroughly tasted. When will the sweet return to the sugarcane realm?
